рд╡рд┐рд╕реНрддрд╛рд░рдГ (рджреНрд░рд╖реНрдЯреБрдВ рдиреЛрджреНрдпрдореН)

IFP manuscript 39691 yogaj─Бgama There are 160 folios in this bundle and 7 or 8 lines per folio. The size of the folio is 17x2 inches. This bundle deals with yogaj─Бgama , which is one of the mul─Бgamas of 28 siddhantha ┼Ыaiv─Бgama. It is only 2nd ─Бgama grouped under ┼Ыivabhda. The ┼Ыrot─Б means, the receivers of this ─Бgama are Sudh─Бkhya, Vibhu, Bhasma from Lord Para┼Ыiva. As per K─Бmik─Бgama, the total number of ┼Ыlokas in this ─Бgama is around one lakh. Yogajatantram is the synonym of Yogja─Бgama. There are five Up─Бgamas, namely T─Бram, Vin─Б┼Ыikhottara, ─Бtmayogam, Santam and Santati. This bundle is not a complete text of Yogaj─Бgma, only few paс╣нalas has been mentioned like pariv─Бrasth─Бpanavidhi, ─Бc─Бryasth─Бpanam, vighne┼Ыasth─Бpanam, liс╣Еgasth─Бpanam, ratnaliс╣Еgasth─Бpanam, pratim─Бlakс╣гaс╣Зam, t─Бlasaс╣Еkhyai, ┼Ы┼лlalakс╣гaс╣Зam, pavitr─Бrohaс╣Зam, maс╣Зс╕Нalavidh─Бnam, phalap─Бkavidhiс╕е, pa├▒c─Бkс╣гaram, vibhavani┼Ыcayam, naivedyavidhiс╕е, agnik─Бryam, kuс╣Зс╕Нalakс╣гaс╣Зam, ┼Ы─Бntihomam, d─лkс╣г─Бlakс╣гaс╣Зam and liс╣Еgalakс╣гaс╣Зam|
